profile-result-card__meta"><p class="profile-result-card__location"></p></div></div></li><div class="description__text description__text--rich"><strong>About the Company</strong><br><br>Our client is a Global Technology at the forefront of innovation, pioneering new business and software architecture to support next generation products and solutions. Their Innovation Hub in Dublin is building an industry-recognized multi-discipline team of experts to tackle real world problems.<br><br><strong>Role Summary</strong><br><br>As a <strong><em>Chief Data Scientist</em></strong>, your knowledge and experience in Artificial Intelligence will be applied to solve challenging real-world problems. Your contribution will also help to create new offerings in the areas of intelligence-driven 4G and 5G network, edge computing, distributed cloud, IoT and other emerging businesses.<br><br><strong>Key Responsibilities:</strong><br><br><ul><li>Lead the AI framework architecture design for ultra-large scale network operation platform. </li><li>Lead the design and implement intelligent operations system, which include working with petabytes of networks data, and demonstrating the root cause analysis system, anomaly detection systems, recommendation engines, etc. based on knowledge graph, active learning algorithms, predictive models, statistical model, deep learning, reinforcement learning and other machine learning algorithms. </li><li>Lead studies and creative usage of new and/or existing data sources. Work with architects to leverage existing data models and build new ones as needed. </li><li>Collaborate with product development teams and partners in Businesses to industrialize machine learning models and solutions including providing source code, workflows and documents </li><li>Lead the development of new and apply/extend existing, concepts, methodologies, techniques for cross functional initiatives </li></ul><br><strong>Skills and Experience</strong><br><br><ul><li>PhD in Computer Science, Artificial Intelligence, Machine Learning, or related field; </li><li>5+ years of Machine Learning experience and successful use cases </li><li>Demonstrated practical understanding of the specification, design, documentation, coding, testing and release of commercial software </li><li>Programming skills in various languages (Python, Scala, Java, R or C++) </li><li>Proven skills in Machine Learning, e.g., linear/logistics regression discriminant analysis, bagging, random forest, Bayesian model, SVM, neural networks, knowledge graph, active learning, etc. </li><li>Strong skills in the use of current state of the art machine learning frameworks such as Scikit-Learn, H2O, Keras, TensorFlow and Spark, etc. </li><li>Ability to lead the implement new algorithms and methodologies from leading open source initiatives and research papers addressing their functionalities, scalability and overall industrialization viability </li><li>Experience with Big Data technologies such as HDFS, HBase, MapReduce, etc </li><li>Strong knowledge in Statistics, e.g., descriptive analysis and supervised and unsupervised analysis </li><li>Problem solving ability and lateral thinking capability; </li><li>Proven ability to work under pressure and with short deadlines to accomplish objectives; </li><li>Ability to communicate effectively with technical and non-technical personnel; </li><li>Entrepreneurial thinking and work ethic.</li></ul></div><ul
